OBJECT Report 16504 Revised Form 27Q
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=03-08-16;
    Time=12:00:00 PM;
    Version List=NAVIN9.00.00.46621;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[ENU=Revised Form 27Q;
               ENN=Revised Form 27Q];
    OnPreReport=VAR
                  Form26Q27QEntry@1500001 : Record 16505;
                  ChallanRegister@1500000 : Record 16504;
                  CompanyInformation@1500004 : Record 79;
                  UpdateChallanDetails@1500002 : Report 13721;
                BEGIN
                  IF CurrentQuarter = 0 THEN
                    ERROR(Text16500);
                  IF FinancialYear = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16501);
                  IF TANloc = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16502);
                  IF PersonName = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16502);
                  IF Designation = '' THEN
                    ERROR(Text16504);
                  IF Date = 0D THEN
                    ERROR(Text16505);
                  IF PANNo = '' THEN
                    ERROR(PANNoEmptyErr);

                  UpdateChallanDetails.UpdateNilChallanEntries(TANloc,CurrentQuarter,FinancialYear,FALSE);

                  ChallanRegister.RESET;
                  ChallanRegister.SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                  IF ChallanRegister.ISEMPTY THEN
                    ERROR(Text16506,'Financial Year');
                  ChallanRegister.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                  IF ChallanRegister.ISEMPTY THEN
                    ERROR(Text16506,'Quarter');
                  ChallanRegister.SETRANGE("T.A.N. No.",TANloc);
                  IF ChallanRegister.FINDSET THEN
                    REPEAT
                      Form26Q27QEntry.RESET;
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                      IF Form26Q27QEntry.ISEMPTY THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'Financial Year');
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                      IF Form26Q27QEntry.ISEMPTY THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'Quarter');
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Form No.",Form26Q27QEntry."Form No."::"27Q");
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("T.A.N. No.",TANloc);
                      IF Form26Q27QEntry.ISEMPTY THEN
                        ERROR(Text16506,'T.A.N No.');
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE(Printed,TRUE);
                      Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Challan Register Entry No.",ChallanRegister."Entry No.");
                      Execute += Form26Q27QEntry.COUNT;
                    UNTIL ChallanRegister.NEXT = 0;

                  IF (CompanyInformation."Company Status" <> CompanyInformation."Company Status"::Government) AND
                     (STRLEN(MobileNo) <> 10)
                  THEN
                    ERROR(Text16519);
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 9960;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table16503;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Entry No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Form No.=FILTER(27Q),
                                       No. of Revision=FILTER(<>0));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                               SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                               SETRANGE("Deductor T.A.N. No.",TANloc);
                               SETRANGE(Revised,TRUE);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  Form26Q27QEntry.RESET;
                                  Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                                  Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                                  Form26Q27QEntry.SETRANGE("T.A.N. No.",TANloc);
                                  Form26Q27QEntry.MODIFYALL(Printed,TRUE);
                                  IF NOT (Filed OR Revised) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF Quarter = Quarter::Q4 THEN
                                    Year := COPYSTR(FORMAT("Assessment Year"),1,4)
                                  ELSE
                                    Year := COPYSTR(FORMAT("Financial Year"),1,4);

                                  IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q1 THEN
                                    MonthName := Text16507
                                  ELSE
                                    IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q2 THEN
                                      MonthName := Text16508
                                    ELSE
                                      IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q3 THEN
                                        MonthName := Text16509
                                      ELSE
                                        IF CurrentQuarter = CurrentQuarter::Q4 THEN
                                          MonthName := Text16510;

                                  State.SETFILTER("State Code for eTDS/TCS","Deductor State");
                                  IF State.FINDFIRST THEN;

                                  IF "Correction-Y" THEN
                                    UpdateDeductorDetails := Text16511
                                  ELSE
                                    UpdateDeductorDetails := Text16512;

                                  // IF "Deductor Category" = "Deductor Category"::"0" THEN
                                  //  DeductorType := Text16513
                                  // ELSE
                                  // DeductorType := Text16514;
                                  DeductorType := "Deductor Category";
                                  Num := 0;
                                  Num2 := 0;
                                  ChallanRegisterEntryNo := 0;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 6267;1   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table16505;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Challan Register Entry No.)
                                 WHERE(Challan Register Entry No.=FILTER(<>0),
                                       Form No.=FILTER(27Q),
                                       No. of Revision=FILTER(<>0));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS("Total TDS Including SHE CESS","TDS Amount",TotalTaxDeducted,"eCESS Amount","SHE Cess Amount",
                                 LastTotalTaxDeducted1);

                               SETRANGE("Financial Year",FinancialYear);
                               SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                               SETRANGE(Revised,TRUE);
                               SETRANGE("T.A.N. No.",TANloc);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  Printed := TRUE;
                                  MODIFY;

                                  IF ChallanRegisterEntryNo <> "Challan Register Entry No." THEN BEGIN
                                    TotalTaxDepo := 0;
                                    Form26Q27QEntries.SETRANGE("Challan Register Entry No.","Challan Register Entry No.");
                                    IF Form26Q27QEntries.FIND('-') THEN
                                      REPEAT
                                        TotalTaxDepo += Form26Q27QEntries."Total TDS Including SHE CESS";
                                      UNTIL Form26Q27QEntries.NEXT = 0 ;

                                    IF CurrentQuarter > 0 THEN BEGIN
                                      TDSAccountingPeriod.SETRANGE("Financial Year for eTDS/TCS",FinancialYear);
                                      IF TDSAccountingPeriod.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                        TDSPeriodSetup.RESET;
                                        TDSPeriodSetup.SETRANGE("No.",TDSAccountingPeriod."No.");
                                        TDSPeriodSetup.SETRANGE(Quarter,CurrentQuarter);
                                        IF TDSPeriodSetup.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                          EndDate := COPYSTR(FORMAT(TDSPeriodSetup."Ending Date"),1,6);
                                          EndDate1 := COPYSTR(FORMAT(TDSPeriodSetup."Ending Date"),7,8);
                                        END;
                                      END;
                                    END;

                                    Num3 := 0;
                                    InvAmt := 0;

                                    "Challan Register".SETRANGE("Challan No.","Challan No.");
                                    IF "Challan Register".FIND('-') THEN;

                                    ChallanRegisterEntryNo := "Challan Register Entry No.";
                                  END;

                                  Rate := "TDS %" + ("TDS %" * "Surcharge %" / 100);
                                  RateAtWhichDeducted := Rate + (Rate * ("eCESS %" + "SHE Cess %") / 100);

                                  TotalTaxDeducted := ("TDS Amount" + "Surcharge Amount" + "eCESS Amount" + "SHE Cess Amount");

                                  Num3 := Num3 + 1;

                                  IF "Concessional Code" = '' THEN
                                    "Concessional Code" := Text16517;

                                  NODNOCCertificateNo.SETRANGE("No.","Party Code");
                                  NODNOCCertificateNo.SETFILTER("Stating Date",'<=%1',"Posting Date");
                                  NODNOCCertificateNo.SETFILTER("Ending Date",'>=%1',"Posting Date");
                                  IF NODNOCCertificateNo.FINDFIRST THEN
                                    IF ("Concessional Code" = 'A') OR ("Concessional Code" = 'B') THEN
                                      CertificateNo := NODNOCCertificateNo."Certificate No.";

                                  IF Mode = 'U' THEN
                                    LastTotalTaxDeducted := "TDS Amount" + "Surcharge Amount" +
                                      "eCESS Amount" + "SHE Cess Amount";

                                  IF "Correction-C9" THEN
                                    UpdateModeForDeductee := Text16518;

                                  IF "Deductee Code" = '1' THEN
                                    DeducteeCode := Text16515
                                  ELSE
                                    DeducteeCode := Text16516;

                                  LastTotalTaxDeducted1 := "Total TDS Including SHE CESS";
                                  IF "Correction-C9" THEN
                                    LastTotalTaxDeducted1 := 0;
                                  InvAmt += ABS("Invoice Amount");
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Quarter=FIELD(Quarter),
                            Financial Year=FIELD(Financial Year) }
